                                        <item>6.1.6ab</item>
                                        <item>SS.6.1.18ab</item>
                                        <item>SS.6.1.21cd</item>
                                        <item>SS.6.1.29cd</item>
                                    </list>
                                    <p>Verse SS.6.1.26 and 27 are not in sequence and mixed up with
                                        each other. Folio no 353r has a few words in the margin
                                        below which I couldn’t find where to add them.</p>
                                </note>
                                <note resp="Madhududan Rimal"> 6.41 from NAK 5-333: the ending of
                                    the chapter is: uttaratantre śoṣacikitsā aṣṭatriṃsattamaḥ
                                    kāyacikitsāyāṃ tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ || So it looks like it is being
                                    called chapter 38, not 41. </note>
                                <note resp="Vandana Lele">

                                <note resp="Vandana Lele">
                                    <list>
                                        <item>1) I have doubt about the chapter number as the
                                            colophon of the manuscript mentions:
                                            "uttaratantre'ṣṭapañcāśattamaḥ kāyacikitsāyāṃ
                                            yonivyāpaccikitsā trayoviṅśatitamo'dhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ ||"
                                            As I have understood it, the above heading is given to
                                            the subject of this mail . I have also marked the same
                                            in the transcription file. Please comment.</item>
                                        <item>2) The folios which I have transcribed i.e 480r:3,
                                            480v, 481r, 481v are not paginated.</item>
                                        <item>3) Missing verses: 6.38.2, 3, 4, 5ab, 5cd, 5, 6, 7,
                                            6.38.30ab, 32cd, 32ef Probably, 6.38.4.1 is left out to
                                            mark in the vulgate copy, like other verses 6.38.3.1,
                                            6.38.2 etc. which are in manuscript. I am not sure about
                                            this observation. In vulgate, verse number 6.38.8.1 is
                                            shown as missing but in manuscript I could not find
                                            different text relating to that for addition. (Here,
                                            also I may be wrong.)</item>
                                        <item>4) Additions: 6.38.3.1, 3.2, 4.1, 5.1, 6.1, 7.1</item>
                                        <item>5) SS. 6.38.8cd, 17 cd , 23cd, 26cd, 27cd - the second
                                            half has different text.</item>
                                        <item>6) SS.6.38.28 ab - the first half has different
                                            text.</item>
                                    </list>
                                </note>
                                <note resp="Vandana Lele"> This adhyaya is numbered 47 in the
                                    vulgate and 44.9 in NAK 5-333 <list>
                                        <item>1) Missing verses: 6.47.2, 6.47.4cd, 6.47.11, 12,
                                            6.47.21ab, 22cd, 23ab, 29cd, 30ab 6.47.54ab, 6.47.65cd,
                                            68cd 6.47.73cd, 75cd, 76, 79ab </item>
                                        <item>2) Additions: 6.47.4a, 4b, 6.47.13a, 13b, 13c, 13d,
                                            13e, 13f, 13,g, 13h, 13i, 13j, 6.47.65a, 66a, 68a
                                            6.47.73a, 73b, 73c, 73d, 73e, 73f, 73g </item>
                                        <item>3) Special Notes: <list>
                                                <item>i) The text of 6.47.4a and 4b added by me is
                                                  intermingled with 6.47.4cd which is shown missing
                                                  by me.</item>
                                                <item>ii) 6.47.20cd - the second half verse has
                                                  different text.</item>
                                                <item> iii) 6.47.38 - the first half verse has
                                                  different text. </item>
                                                <item>iv) 6.47.43cd and 44ab - the text is
                                                  intermingled i.e. 43.cd has only a word whereas
                                                  44ab has rest of the text.</item>
                                                <item>v) The Letter-numerals given on the folios are
                                                  not noted by me in the transcription. </item>
                                            </list>
                                        </item>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.17.96">dṛṣṭair ataḥ prasādārtham añjane śṛ<lb n="6"/>ṇu me śubhe
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         meṣaśṛṅgyās tu puṣpāṇi śirīṣadhavayor api || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.17.97"> jātyāś caiva hi tulyāṇi muktā vaiḍūryam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         ajākṣīreṇa sampiṣya tāmre saptāham āvapet || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.17.98"> varttīs tās tu<pb n="375r"/> tataḥ kṛtvā yojayed añjane
                        bhiṣak | <!-\-DSCN3350  -\->
                        <caesura/>
                         srotojaṃ vidrumaṃ phenaḥ sāgarasya manaḥśilā || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.17.99"> maricāni ca tā vartī kārayed vāpi pūrvvavat |
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛṣṭeḥ sthairyam etāstha vidadhyā<lb n="2"/>d añjane hitā || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.17.100">bhūyo vakṣyāmi mukhyāni vistareṇāñjanāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kalpe nānāprakārāṇi tāny apīha prayojayed iti ||</l>
                </div>
                <!-\- end of chapter 17 of uttaratantra -\->

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.1"> athātaḥ karṇṇagatarogavijñānīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.5"> ete karṇṇagatā rogā<metamark function="yati">,</metamark>
                        viṃśad aṣṭau <lb n="3"/>ca kīrttitāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.6"> samīraṇaḥ śrotragato 'nyathācaran samantata<cb/>ḥ śūlam
                        atīva karṇṇayoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         karoti doṣaiś ca yathāśvam āvṛtaḥ sa karṇṇaśūlaḥ kathito durāsadaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.7">
                        <lb n="4"/>yadā ca tiṣṭhet tu vimārggam āgataḥ same<add place="bottom
                            margin">tya<metamark
                                function="line_number_from_bottom">3</metamark></add> nāḍīṃ
                        sahaśabdavāhi<cb/>nīṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śṛṇoti śabdān vividhān tathā naraḥ praṇādam enaṃ kathayanti cāmayaṃ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.8"> sa eva śabdābhiva<lb n="5"/>hāḥ sirā yadā<metamark
                            function="yati">,</metamark> kaphānuyāto vyanusṛtya tiṣṭhati |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadā nara<cb/>sya pratikārasevino<metamark function="yati">,</metamark>
                        bhaved dhi bādhiryam asaṃśayaṃ khalu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.9"> śramāklamād vāpi hi rūkṣabhojinaḥ sa<lb n="6"/><g
                            ref="#newa-placeholder-mark"/>mīraṇaḥ śabdapathe vyavasthitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viriktamūrddhasya narasya dāruṇaṃ karoti hi kṣvelam atīva karṇṇayoḥ ||<g
                            ref="#newa-placeholder-mark"/>
                    </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.10">
                        <pb n="381v"/><lb n="1"/>śirobhighātād athavā nimajjato jale prapākād
                        athavāpi vidradheḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sraved dhi pūyaṃ khalu yatra karṇṇataḥ sa karṇṇasaṃsrāva iti prakīrttitaḥ
                            ||<g ref="#newa-placeholder-mark"/>
                    </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.11">
                        <lb n="2"/>kaphena kaṇḍūpacitena karṇṇayo<del rend="crossed out">ḥ</del>r
                        bbhṛśam bhavet srotasi kaṇḍusaṃjñi<cb/>taḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśoṣite śleṣmaṇi pittatejasā dhruvam bhavet srotasi karṇṇagūthakaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.12"> sa karṇṇagūtho dravatāṃ ya<lb n="3"/>dā gato vilāpito
                        ghrāṇasukhaṃ prapadyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadā sa karṇṇapra<cb/>tināhasaṃjñito bhaved vikāraḥ śiraso 'nuvedakṛt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.13"> yadā tu mūrcchanty athavāpi jantavaḥ sṛjanty a<lb n="4"
                        />patyāny athavāpi makṣikā<metamark function="yati">,</metamark> |
                        <caesura/>
                         tadañjanatvāc chravaṇo nirudhya<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><cb/>te
                        bhiṣagbhir ādyaiḥ krimikarṇṇa ity atha || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.14"> kṣatābhighātaprabhavas tu vidradhi<metamark
                            function="yati">,</metamark>r bbhavet tathā doṣakṛto paraḥ <lb n="5"
                        />punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saraktapītāruṇam asram āsravet pratodadhūmāyanadāha<cb/>coṣavān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.15"> bhavet prapākaḥ khalu pittakopato<metamark
                            function="yati">,</metamark> vikothavikledakaras tu karṇṇayoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         srotrasthite śle<lb n="6"/>ṣmaṇi pittatejasā vilīyamāne bhṛśasaṃpratāpitaḥ
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.6.20.16"> avedano vāpy athavā rujānvito ghanaṃ sravet
                        pūtikapūtikarṇṇataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratiṣṭaliṃgāny arśāṃsi yatnata<del rend="crossed out">ḥ</del>s tathaiva
                            śophā<pb n="382r"/>rbbudaliṃgam īritam iti || ❈ ||</l>


                    <p ana="trailer">śālākye karṇṇagatarogavijñānīyam ekonaviṃśatitamo dhyāyaḥ || ❈

                        <caesura/>

                <!--Uttaratantra 6.44-->
                <div n="44" type="adhyāya">
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.1"><pb n="3422V"/>
                        <lb n="1"/>athātaḥ pāṇḍurpgapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.2">vyāyāmamamlaṃ lavaṇāni madyaṃ mṛdaṃ divāsvapnamatīva
                        tīkṣṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         niṣevyamāṇasya vidūṣya raktaṃ kurvvanti doṣāstvaci pāṇḍubhāvaṃ ||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.3">pāṇdvā<lb n="2"/>mayoṣṭārddhavidhaḥ pradiṣṭaḥ
                        pṛthaksamastair yugapac ca doṣaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvve<cb/>ṣu caivaṣvihapāṇḍabhāvo yato 'dhikotaḥ khalu pāṇḍurogaḥ ||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.6.44.4">tvaksphoṭaṣṭhīvanagātrasāda mṛdbhakṣaṇa<lb n="3"
                        />prekṣaṇakūṭaśothāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viṇmūtrapītatvamathāvipāko bhaviṣya<cb/>tastasya puras sarāṇi ||</l>

                        <caesura/>

                        kāyacikitsāyāṃ saptamaḥ || ||</p>
